# Data Broker Opt-Out Directory

A catalogue of **856 data brokers** and how to remove yourself from each, built by automated scouting and verified opt-out paths. 723 have a confirmed opt-out flow.

> You are your own agent here. Pick a broker, open its opt-out page, and follow the steps. Brokers marked *find your listing first* require you to search your name on their site before requesting removal. 19 require a photo ID.

**Legend:** sensitivity is a rough 1-10 estimate of how invasive the data is. *blocked* means our scanner hit an anti-bot wall; the page usually still works in a normal browser.

## Contents

- [People Search Site](#people-search-site) (266)
- [Marketing](#marketing) (129)
- [Risk Mitigation](#risk-mitigation) (10)
- [Recruitment](#recruitment) (5)
- [Unknown](#unknown) (446)


## People Search Site

#### [Alabama People Records](https://alabamapeoplerecords.org/opt-out)
`alabamapeoplerecords.org` · People Search Site · sensitivity 4/10
- **Opt out via web form:** [open the opt-out page](https://alabamapeoplerecords.org/opt-out)
- difficulty: medium · ID required: no · find your listing first: yes · email confirmation: unknown
- **Steps:** Direct access - form is immediately visible on the opt-out landing page
- *Status: verified, last checked 2026-06-01*
